            window.nsglibCommon = window.nsglibCommon || {};

window.nsglibCommon.gemius = (function() {

    var inserted = false;
    var defaultGemiusId = null;

    return {
        hit : hit,
        logInserted : logInserted,
        logDefaultId : logDefaultId
    };

    function logDefaultId(gemiusId) {

        defaultGemiusId = gemiusId;
    }

    function logInserted() {

        inserted = true;
    }

    function hit(gemiusId) {

        if (inserted === false) {
            insertGemius();
        }

        if (typeof (gemius_hit) === 'function') {

            if (typeof gemiusId !== 'undefined') {

                gemius_hit(gemiusId);

            } else if (defaultGemiusId) {

                gemius_hit(defaultGemiusId);

            } else {

                console.log('+ gemius -> brak zdefiniowanego gemius id');
            }
        } else {
            console.log('brak funkcji gemius_hit');
        }
    }

    function insertGemius() {

        inserted = true;

        function gemius_pending(i) {
            window[i] = window[i] || function() {
                var x = window[i + '_pdata'] = window[i + '_pdata'] || [];
                x[x.length] = arguments;
            };
        }

        gemius_pending('gemius_hit');
        gemius_pending('gemius_event');
        gemius_pending('pp_gemius_hit');
        gemius_pending('pp_gemius_event');

        (function(d, t) {
            try {
                var gt = d.createElement(t),
                    s = d.getElementsByTagName(t)[0],
                    l = 'http' + ((location.protocol == 'https:') ? 's' : '');
                gt.setAttribute('async', 'async');
                gt.setAttribute('defer', 'defer');
                gt.src = l + '://onet.hit.gemius.pl/xgemius.js';
                s.parentNode.insertBefore(gt, s);
            } catch (e) {}
        })(document, 'script');

    }
})();
        window.store.initObserver('1500')
